The collaboration, co-written by the duo with Tito Laija and Grammy-winning producer <a href="/wiki/Edgar_Barrera" title="Edgar Barrera">Edgar Barrera</a>, narrates the story of a failed relationship.<sup id="cite_ref-:28_192-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:28-192">&#91;192&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-:29_193-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:29-193">&#91;193&#93;</a></sup> On April 1, she opened the pinnacle event of the <a href="/wiki/WWE" title="WWE">WWE</a>, <a href="/wiki/WrestleMania_39" title="WrestleMania 39">WrestleMania 39</a>, performing "<a href="/wiki/America_the_Beautiful" title="America the Beautiful">America the Beautiful</a>".<sup id="cite_ref-194" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-194">&#91;194&#93;</a></sup> On April 14 and 21, Gomez performed at the <a href="/wiki/Coachella_(festival)" title="Coachella (festival)">Coachella Valley Music and Arts Festival</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-195" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-195">&#91;195&#93;</a></sup> On May 9, Gomez announced her first headlining tour, titled <a href="/wiki/Mi_Casa,_Tu_Casa_Tour" title="Mi Casa, Tu Casa Tour">Mi Casa, Tu Casa Tour</a>. It is set to begin in <a href="/wiki/Boston" title="Boston">Boston</a>, <a href="/wiki/Massachusetts" title="Massachusetts">Massachusetts</a>, on September 14, and visit several cities in the United States.<sup id="cite_ref-196" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-196">&#91;196&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-197" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-197">&#91;197&#93;</a></sup> On May 12, she was featured in a remix of "<a href="/wiki/I_Ain%27t_Worried" title="I Ain&#39;t Worried">I Ain't Worried</a>" by American band <a href="/wiki/OneRepublic" title="OneRepublic">OneRepublic</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-198" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-198">&#91;198&#93;</a></sup> On June 2, Gomez released song "The Fire Inside" from the <i><a href="/wiki/Flamin%27_Hot" title="Flamin&#39; Hot">Flamin' Hot</a></i> film soundtrack.<sup id="cite_ref-199" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-199">&#91;199&#93;</a></sup> On June 2, she released the song "Take It To The Top" with Nigerian singer <a href="/wiki/Ayra_Starr" title="Ayra Starr">Ayra Starr</a>, from the deluxe edition of the American computer-animated superhero film <i><a href="/wiki/Spider-Man:_Across_the_Spider-Verse" title="Spider-Man: Across the Spider-Verse">Spider-Man: Across the Spider-Verse</a></i> soundtrack.<sup id="cite_ref-:0_200-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-200">&#91;200&#93;</a></sup> On June 28, Gomez released the single "<a href="/wiki/La_Nena_(song)" title="La Nena (song)">La Nena</a>" with Mexican singer Gabito Ballesteros, as the second single for her upcoming regional Mexican album.<sup id="cite_ref-201" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-201">&#91;201&#93;</a></sup> On July 20, Nigerian singer <a href="/wiki/Kizz_Daniel" title="Kizz Daniel">Kizz Daniel</a> released the single "Cough" with Gomez.<sup id="cite_ref-202" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-202">&#91;202&#93;</a></sup> On August 16, Haitian DJ <a href="/wiki/Micha%C3%ABl_Brun" title="Michaël Brun">Michaël Brun</a> released the single "Coming Your Way" with Gomez and English singer <a href="/wiki/Anne-Marie" title="Anne-Marie">Anne-Marie</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-203" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-203">&#91;203&#93;</a></sup> Gomez voices Khaji-Da, an entity inside <a href="/wiki/Jaime_Reyes" class="mw-redirect" title="Jaime Reyes">Jaime Reyes</a>' Scarab, in the <a href="/wiki/DC_Studios" title="DC Studios">DC Studios</a> film <i><a href="/wiki/Blue_Beetle_(film)" title="Blue Beetle (film)">Blue Beetle</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-204" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-204">&#91;204&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>On August 25, Gomez announced her upcoming third studio album <i><a href="/wiki/Esquinas_(album)" title="Esquinas (album)">Esquinas</a></i>, expected to be released sometime in late 2023. The album will be <a href="/wiki/Regional_Mexican" title="Regional Mexican">Regional Mexican</a>, her first in the genre, as a tribute to her grandparents, who emigrated from Mexico to the United States. Explaining its title, Gomez stated:
</p>
<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r996844942"><blockquote class="templatequote"><p>“I have always identified as not this side or that side of the streets that raised me, but the corner where two flags, two cultures, two languages meet.”<sup id="cite_ref-205" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-205">&#91;205&#93;</a></sup></p></blockquote>
<p>On September 14, Gomez released the single "Querido Abuelo". The single is dedicated to her grandfather who died in 2021.<sup id="cite_ref-206" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-206">&#91;206&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Artistry">Artistry</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Becky_G&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Artistry">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Gomez is described as a <a href="/wiki/Hip_hop_music" title="Hip hop music">hip hop</a>, <a href="/wiki/Pop_rap" title="Pop rap">pop rap</a>, <a href="/wiki/Pop_music" title="Pop music">pop</a>, <a href="/wiki/Latin_music" title="Latin music">latin</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Reggaeton" title="Reggaeton">reggaeton</a> artist.<sup id="cite_ref-207" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-207">&#91;207&#93;</a></sup> Her debut studio album is a <a href="/wiki/Latin_pop" title="Latin pop">Latin pop</a> and <a href="/wiki/Reggaeton" title="Reggaeton">reggaeton</a> record, incorporating elements of <a href="/wiki/Latin_hip_hop" title="Latin hip hop">Latin hip hop</a> and <a href="/wiki/Urbano_music" title="Urbano music">urbano</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-208" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-208">&#91;208&#93;</a></sup> Her second album followed close, although focusing more on <a href="/wiki/Dance-pop" title="Dance-pop">dance-pop</a> and <a href="/wiki/Rhythm_and_blues" title="Rhythm and blues">R&amp;B</a> sounds. Her upcoming third studio album will be focused on <a href="/wiki/Regional_styles_of_Mexican_music" title="Regional styles of Mexican music">Mexican Regional music</a>, a nod to her Mexican roots. Gomez is known for her versatility, often collaborating with different artists from different genres, such as <a href="/wiki/Country_music" title="Country music">country</a>, <a href="/wiki/Electronic_music" title="Electronic music">EDM</a>, <a href="/wiki/K-pop" title="K-pop">K-pop</a>, <a href="/wiki/Funk_carioca" title="Funk carioca">funk</a>, among others.
</p><p>Gomez has cited late Tejano singer <a href="/wiki/Selena" title="Selena">Selena</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-209" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-209">&#91;209&#93;</a></sup> American singer and actress <a href="/wiki/Jennifer_Lopez" title="Jennifer Lopez">Jennifer Lopez</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-210" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-210">&#91;210&#93;</a></sup> Mexican singer and actress <a href="/wiki/Thal%C3%ADa" title="Thalía">Thalía</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-211" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-211">&#91;211&#93;</a></sup> late Mexican American banda singer-songwriter <a href="/wiki/Jenni_Rivera" title="Jenni Rivera">Jenni Rivera</a>, Colombian singer-songwriter <a href="/wiki/Shakira" title="Shakira">Shakira</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-212" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-212">&#91;212&#93;</a></sup> American singer <a href="/wiki/Christina_Aguilera" title="Christina Aguilera">Christina Aguilera</a>, and Brazilian singer <a href="/wiki/Anitta_(singer)" title="Anitta (singer)">Anitta</a><sup id="cite_ref-213" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-213">&#91;213&#93;</a></sup> as influences.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Products_and_endorsements">Products and endorsements</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Becky_G&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Products and endorsements">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Gomez began representing <a href="/wiki/CoverGirl" title="CoverGirl">CoverGirl</a> in July 2014.<sup id="cite_ref-covergirl_214-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-covergirl-214">&#91;214&#93;</a></sup> As the spokeswoman for the company, she filmed commercials to promote the brand and featured their products in her music videos.<sup id="cite_ref-covergirl_214-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-covergirl-214">&#91;214&#93;</a></sup> In December 2018, Gomez released a makeup collection called <i>Salvaje</i> with cosmetics brand <a href="/wiki/ColourPop" class="mw-redirect" title="ColourPop">ColourPop</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-215" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-215">&#91;215&#93;</a></sup> In March 2021, Gomez collaborated with <a href="/wiki/PrettyLittleThing" title="PrettyLittleThing">PrettyLittleThing</a>, creating the Streetwear Pieces Collection.<sup id="cite_ref-216" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-216">&#91;216&#93;</a></sup> In June, Gomez launched her makeup line, Treslúce Beauty, which is distributed by <a href="/wiki/Ulta_Beauty" title="Ulta Beauty">Ulta Beauty</a> as of March 2022.<sup id="cite_ref-217" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-217">&#91;217&#93;</a></sup> In 2023, Gomez collaborated with Patron Tequila.<sup id="cite_ref-218" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-218">&#91;218&#93;</a></sup> In June, Gomez joined swimwear brand Gonza as new creative director.<sup id="cite_ref-219" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-219">&#91;219&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personal_life">Personal life</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Becky_G&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Personal life">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Gomez dated American singer <a href="/wiki/Austin_Mahone" title="Austin Mahone">Austin Mahone</a> from February to August in 2015.<sup id="cite_ref-220" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-220">&#91;220&#93;</a></sup> In June 2016, it was confirmed that Gomez was in a relationship with American professional soccer player <a href="/wiki/Sebastian_Lletget" title="Sebastian Lletget">Sebastian Lletget</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-221" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-221">&#91;221&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-222" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-222">&#91;222&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-223" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-223">&#91;223&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-224" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-224">&#91;224&#93;</a></sup> The couple announced their engagement on December 9, 2022.<sup id="cite_ref-225" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-225">&#91;225&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-226" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-226">&#91;226&#93;</a></sup> Lleget apologized for cheating allegations in late March 2023.<sup id="cite_ref-227" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-227">&#91;227&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-228" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-228">&#91;228&#93;</a></sup> No further statements from either parties have been issued.
</p><p>While on tour with <a href="/wiki/Fifth_Harmony" title="Fifth Harmony">Fifth Harmony</a> in October 2017, Gomez suffered an "out-of-control fan attack" while in <a href="/wiki/Mexico_City" title="Mexico City">Mexico City</a>. Gomez took to <a href="/wiki/Snapchat" title="Snapchat">Snapchat</a> to speak about the incident and also revealed that she had been dealing with anxiety issues.<sup id="cite_ref-229" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-229">&#91;229&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-230" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-230">&#91;230&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Achievements">Achievements</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Becky_G&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Achievements">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1033289096"><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Becky_G" title="List of awards and nominations received by Becky G">List of awards and nominations received by Becky G</a></div>
<p>Gomez has won an <a href="/wiki/IHeartRadio_Music_Awards" title="IHeartRadio Music Awards">iHeartRadio Music Award</a>, nine <a href="/wiki/Latin_American_Music_Awards" title="Latin American Music Awards">Latin American Music Awards</a>, and three <a href="/wiki/People%27s_Choice_Awards" title="People&#39;s Choice Awards">People's Choice Awards</a>. She has been nominated for a <a href="/wiki/Billboard_Music_Awards" title="Billboard Music Awards">Billboard Music Award</a> and six <a href="/wiki/Latin_Grammy_Awards" title="Latin Grammy Awards">Latin Grammy Award</a>. 
</p><p>Gomez was honored as one of the <a href="/wiki/Leading_Ladies_of_Entertainment" title="Leading Ladies of Entertainment">Leading Ladies of Entertainment</a> by <a href="/wiki/The_Latin_Recording_Academy" title="The Latin Recording Academy">The Latin Recording Academy</a> in 2018.<sup id="cite_ref-latinacademy_95-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-latinacademy-95">&#91;95&#93;</a></sup> In 2019, Gomez was awarded the <a href="/wiki/Latin_American_Music_Awards_of_2019" title="Latin American Music Awards of 2019">Extraordinary Evolution Award</a> for her evolving work in a short span of years.<sup id="cite_ref-extraordinaryevolutionaward_121-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-extraordinaryevolutionaward-121">&#91;121&#93;</a></sup> Gomez was named to <i><a href="/wiki/Forbes" title="Forbes">Forbes</a>'</i> <a href="/wiki/30_Under_30" class="mw-redirect" title="30 Under 30">30 Under 30</a> list in the music category.<sup id="cite_ref-forbeslist_186-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-forbeslist-186">&#91;186&#93;</a></sup> In 2023, she received the <a href="/wiki/Billboard_Women_in_Music#Impact_Award" title="Billboard Women in Music">Impact Award</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Billboard_Women_in_Music" title="Billboard Women in Music"><i>Billboard</i> Women in Music</a> event.<sup id="cite_ref-billboardimpact_188-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-billboardimpact-188">&#91;188&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Discography">Discography</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Becky_G&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Discography">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1033289096"><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main articles: <a href="/wiki/Becky_G_discography" title="Becky G discography">Becky G discography</a> and <a href="/wiki/List_of_songs_recorded_by_Becky_G" title="List of songs recorded by Becky G">List of songs recorded by Becky G</a></div>

<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1033289096"><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Becky_G_videography" title="Becky G videography">Becky G videography</a></div>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Tours">Tours</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Becky_G&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Tours">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1033289096"><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/List_of_Becky_G_live_performances" title="List of Becky G live performances">List of Becky G live performances</a></div>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="References">References</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Becky_G&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: References">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
